â€“ PKG çš„å…¬é’¥ğ¾ =ğ‘”ğ‘

(a) p=3, q=11, e = 7, M = 5
n = p Ã— q = 33; e = 7; M = 5; Ï†(n) = 2 Ã— 10 = 20; e Ã— d mod 20 = 1; hence d = 3
Encryption:
C = M^e mod n = 5^7 mod 33 = 14
Decryption
M = C^d mod n = 14^3 mod 33 = 5 = M

(ä¸ºäº†ä½¿å®šç†æœ‰æ•ˆï¼Œç»„ä¸­çš„æ‰€æœ‰å…ƒç´ å¿…é¡»æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªä¹˜æ³•é€†ï¼Œå³ã€‚ Gcd(a,p)=1)

å¯¹äºç¡¬ä»¶ï¼šåŠ å‡çš„ç›¸å…³æ¶æ„æ˜¯ï¼šRipple Carry, Carry Lookahead, Carry Save, Carry Select Î® Carry Skip adders

è’™å“¥é©¬åˆ©æ¨¡ä¹˜æ³•ï¼ˆMontM(x,y,p) å‡½æ•°ï¼‰

è¾“å…¥ï¼š$ x = {x_{n-1},â€¦,x_2, x_1, x_0 }b < p,\ y = {y{n-1},â€¦,y_2, y_1 , y_0 }b < p,\ p = {p{n-1},â€¦, p_1, p_0 }_b,\ r = b^n, p^\prime = -p^{-1} \mod b$ b: ä¸€ä¸ªå¸¸æ•°ï¼ˆé€šå¸¸æ˜¯ 2 çš„å¹‚ï¼‰
è¾“å‡ºï¼š$c = x \cdot y \cdot r^{-1} \mod p$

  1. c = 0
  2. å¯¹äº i=0 åˆ° n-1 åš
    2.1. $q=(c_0+x_i\cdot y_0)p^\prime \mod b$
    2.2. $c=\frac{c+x_i\cdot y+q\cdot p}{b}$
  3. å¦‚æœ $c \ge p$ é‚£ä¹ˆ c = c â€“ p
  4. è¿”å› c.

è’™å“¥é©¬åˆ©åŸŸ

æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­— $X_R = X â‹… ğ‘Ÿ \mod ğ‘$ï¼Œè€Œä¸æ˜¯æ•°å­— X

åœ¨è’™å“¥é©¬åˆ©åŸŸä¸­çš„æ•°å­—ä¹‹é—´æ‰§è¡Œè’™å“¥é©¬åˆ©ä¹˜æ³•äº§ç”Ÿä¹Ÿåœ¨è’™å“¥é©¬åˆ©åŸŸä¸­çš„ç»“æœ

æ¨¡å¹‚ç®—æ³• Modular Exponentiation Algorithm

è¾“å…¥ï¼šg in G and x>0 ; è¾“å‡ºï¼š G ä¸­çš„ $g^x$
è¡¨ç¤º $x = (x_n x_{n-1} â€¦ x_2 x_1 x_0)_2$

ä¾‹å¦‚

é«˜æ•ˆçš„æ¨¡å¹‚ç®—æ³•

è’™å“¥é©¬åˆ©æ¨¡å¹‚ï¼ˆMontMexp(x,e,p) å‡½æ•°ï¼‰

è¾“å…¥ï¼š$ x = {x_{n-1},â€¦,x_2, x_1, x_0 }2 < p,\ y = {y{n-1},â€¦,y_2, y_1 , y_0 }2 < p,\ p = {p{n-1},â€¦, p_1, p_0 }_2,\ r = b^n $ ï¼ˆé€šå¸¸ b=2 æˆ– 2 çš„å¹‚ï¼‰
è¾“å‡ºï¼š$c = x^e \mod p$

  1. $ c= r\mod p $
  2. $g = r^2 \mod p $
  3. $\bar{x} = x \cdot g \cdot r^{-1} \mod p $
  4. For i in (n-1) to 0:
    1. $c = c \cdot c \cdot r^{-1} \mod p $
    2. if $e_i = 1$ then $c=c\cdot \bar{x} \cdot r^{-1} \mod p$
  5. $ c =c \cdot 1 \cdot r^{-1} \mod p$

Using Fermatâ€™s theorem, find 3^2001 mod 11

Fermatâ€™s Theorem states
if p is prime and a is a positive integer not divisible by p, then a^{pâˆ’1} mod p â‰¡ 1. Therefore 3^10 mod 11 â‰¡ 1.
Therefore 3^2001 = (3^10)^200 Ã— 3 mod 11 = 1 Ã— 3 mod 11 = 3

Using Multiplicative inverses Fermat little Theorem, find the multiplicative inverse of 3 mod 5?
The multiplicative inverse of 3 mod 5 is 3^{-1} mod 5 = 3^{5-2} mod 5
Therefore 3^3 mod 5 = 27 mod 5 = 2

Using Multiplicative inverses Fermat little Theorem, find the multiplicative inverse of 8 mod 17?
8^{-1} mod 17
8^{17-2} mod 17 = 8^15 mod 17 = 8^7 * 8^8 mod 17 = 15 * 1 mod 17 = 15
